auth, gzip bool, methods ...string) (route *mux.Route) {\n164: \t// Propagate the consistency level on all HTTP routes.\n165: \t// They are not used everywhere, but for consistency and less surprise it's added everywhere.\n166: \thandler = propagation.Middleware(&querierapi.ConsistencyExtractor{}).Wrap(handler)\n167: \n168: \tif auth {\n169: \t\thandler = a.AuthMiddleware.Wrap(handler)\n170: \t}\n171: \tif gzip {\n172: \t\thandler = gziphandler.GzipHandler(handler)\n173: \t}\n174: \tif isPrefix {\n175: \t\troute = a.server.HTTP.PathPrefix(path)\n176: \t} else {\n177: \t\troute = a.server.HTTP.Path(path)\n178: \t}\n179: \tif len(methods) > 0 {\n180: \t\troute = route.Methods(methods...)\n181: \t}\n182: \troute = route.Handler(handler)\n183: \n184: \treturn route\n185: }\n186:
